\section{External states: ${e_{{i}}, \bar{e}_{{j}}, e_{{k}}, \bar{e}_{{l}}}$} 
\subsection{Wave contributions, Propagator: $h$}

\begin{align} 
I_1= & B_0(0, m^2_{e_{{b}}}, m^2_{A^0_{{a}}}) \\ 
I_2= & B_1(0, m^2_{e_{{b}}}, m^2_{A^0_{{a}}}) \\ 
  PSO4lSLL= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,L}_{j, c, p} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,L}_{l, k, p} \frac{1}{m^2_{h_{{p}}}} (-(\Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{c, b, a} I_2 m^2_{e_{{i}}}) + \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{c, b, a} I_1 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{b}}} - \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{c, b, a} I_2 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{c}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{c, b, a} I_1 m_{e_{{b}}} m_{e_{{c}}}))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PSO4lSRR= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,R}_{j, c, p} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,R}_{l, k, p} \frac{1}{m^2_{h_{{p}}}} (-(\Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{c, b, a} I_2 m^2_{e_{{i}}}) + \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{c, b, a} I_1 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{b}}} - \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{c, b, a} I_2 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{c}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{c, b, a} I_1 m_{e_{{b}}} m_{e_{{c}}}))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PSO4lSRL= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,R}_{j, c, p} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,L}_{l, k, p} \frac{1}{m^2_{h_{{p}}}} (-(\Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{c, b, a} I_2 m^2_{e_{{i}}}) + \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{c, b, a} I_1 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{b}}} - \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{c, b, a} I_2 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{c}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{c, b, a} I_1 m_{e_{{b}}} m_{e_{{c}}}))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PSO4lSLR= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,L}_{j, c, p} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,R}_{l, k, p} \frac{1}{m^2_{h_{{p}}}} (-(\Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{c, b, a} I_2 m^2_{e_{{i}}}) + \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{c, b, a} I_1 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{b}}} - \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,R}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{c, b, a} I_2 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{c}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{b, i, a} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e A^0 ,L}_{c, b, a} I_1 m_{e_{{b}}} m_{e_{{c}}}))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PSO4lVRR= & 0 \\ 
  PSO4lVLL= & 0 \\ 
  PSO4lVRL= & 0 \\ 
  PSO4lVLR= & 0 \\ 
  PSO4lTLL= & 0 \\ 
  PSO4lTLR= & 0 \\ 
  PSO4lTRL= & 0 \\ 
  PSO4lTRR= & 0 \\ 
\end{align}

  PSO4lSLL= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,L}_{j, c, p} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,L}_{l, k, p} \frac{1}{m^2_{h_{{p}}}} (-(\Gamma^{e e \delta^{c++},L}_{i, a, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\bar{e}\delta^{c--} ,R}_{c, a, b} I_2 m^2_{e_{{i}}}) + \Gamma^{e e \delta^{c++},R}_{i, a, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\bar{e}\delta^{c--} ,R}_{c, a, b} I_1 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{a}}} - \Gamma^{e e \delta^{c++},R}_{i, a, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\bar{e}\delta^{c--} ,L}_{c, a, b} I_2 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{c}}} + \Gamma^{e e \delta^{c++},L}_{i, a, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\bar{e}\delta^{c--} ,L}_{c, a, b} I_1 m_{e_{{a}}} m_{e_{{c}}}))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PSO4lSRR= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,R}_{j, c, p} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,R}_{l, k, p} \frac{1}{m^2_{h_{{p}}}} (-(\Gamma^{e e \delta^{c++},R}_{i, a, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\bar{e}\delta^{c--} ,L}_{c, a, b} I_2 m^2_{e_{{i}}}) + \Gamma^{e e \delta^{c++},L}_{i, a, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\bar{e}\delta^{c--} ,L}_{c, a, b} I_1 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{a}}} - \Gamma^{e e \delta^{c++},L}_{i, a, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\bar{e}\delta^{c--} ,R}_{c, a, b} I_2 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{c}}} + \Gamma^{e e \delta^{c++},R}_{i, a, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\bar{e}\delta^{c--} ,R}_{c, a, b} I_1 m_{e_{{a}}} m_{e_{{c}}}))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PSO4lSRL= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,R}_{j, c, p} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,L}_{l, k, p} \frac{1}{m^2_{h_{{p}}}} (-(\Gamma^{e e \delta^{c++},R}_{i, a, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\bar{e}\delta^{c--} ,L}_{c, a, b} I_2 m^2_{e_{{i}}}) + \Gamma^{e e \delta^{c++},L}_{i, a, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\bar{e}\delta^{c--} ,L}_{c, a, b} I_1 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{a}}} - \Gamma^{e e \delta^{c++},L}_{i, a, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\bar{e}\delta^{c--} ,R}_{c, a, b} I_2 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{c}}} + \Gamma^{e e \delta^{c++},R}_{i, a, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\bar{e}\delta^{c--} ,R}_{c, a, b} I_1 m_{e_{{a}}} m_{e_{{c}}}))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PSO4lSLR= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,L}_{j, c, p} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,R}_{l, k, p} \frac{1}{m^2_{h_{{p}}}} (-(\Gamma^{e e \delta^{c++},L}_{i, a, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\bar{e}\delta^{c--} ,R}_{c, a, b} I_2 m^2_{e_{{i}}}) + \Gamma^{e e \delta^{c++},R}_{i, a, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\bar{e}\delta^{c--} ,R}_{c, a, b} I_1 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{a}}} - \Gamma^{e e \delta^{c++},R}_{i, a, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\bar{e}\delta^{c--} ,L}_{c, a, b} I_2 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{c}}} + \Gamma^{e e \delta^{c++},L}_{i, a, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\bar{e}\delta^{c--} ,L}_{c, a, b} I_1 m_{e_{{a}}} m_{e_{{c}}}))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\ 
  PSO4lVRR= & 0 \\ 
  PSO4lVLL= & 0 \\ 
  PSO4lVRL= & 0 \\ 
  PSO4lVLR= & 0 \\

  PSO4lSRR= & ( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,R}_{j, c, p} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,R}_{l, k, p} \frac{1}{m^2_{h_{{p}}}} (-(\Gamma^{\nu e H^+,R}_{a, i, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu H^- ,L}_{c, a, b} I_2 m^2_{e_{{i}}}) + \Gamma^{\nu e H^+,L}_{a, i, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu H^- ,L}_{c, a, b} I_1 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{\nu_{{a}}} - \Gamma^{\nu e H^+,L}_{a, i, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu H^- ,R}_{c, a, b} I_2 m_{e_{{i}}} m_{e_{{c}}} + \Gamma^{\nu e H^+,R}_{a, i, b} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu H^- ,R}_{c, a, b} I_1 m_{\nu_{{a}}} m_{e_{{c}}}))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}}) \\

\begin{align} 
I_1= & B_0(0, m^2_{\nu_{{a}}}, m^2_{W^-}) \\ 
I_2= & B_1(0, m^2_{\nu_{{a}}}, m^2_{W^-}) \\ 
  PSO4lSLL= & -(( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,L}_{j, c, p} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,L}_{l, k, p} \frac{1}{m^2_{h_{{p}}}} (\Gamma^{\nu e W^+,R}_{a, i} m_{e_{{i}}} (-2 \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^- ,L}_{c, a} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{\nu_{{a}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^- ,R}_{c, a} (1 + 2 I_2) m_{e_{{c}}}) + \Gamma^{\nu e W^+,L}_{a, i} (\Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^- ,L}_{c, a} (1 + 2 I_2) m^2_{e_{{i}}} - 2 \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^- ,R}_{c, a} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{\nu_{{a}}} m_{e_{{c}}})))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}})) \\ 
  PSO4lSRR= & -(( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,R}_{j, c, p} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,R}_{l, k, p} \frac{1}{m^2_{h_{{p}}}} (\Gamma^{\nu e W^+,L}_{a, i} m_{e_{{i}}} (-2 \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^- ,R}_{c, a} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{\nu_{{a}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^- ,L}_{c, a} (1 + 2 I_2) m_{e_{{c}}}) + \Gamma^{\nu e W^+,R}_{a, i} (\Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^- ,R}_{c, a} (1 + 2 I_2) m^2_{e_{{i}}} - 2 \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^- ,L}_{c, a} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{\nu_{{a}}} m_{e_{{c}}})))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}})) \\ 
  PSO4lSRL= & -(( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,R}_{j, c, p} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,L}_{l, k, p} \frac{1}{m^2_{h_{{p}}}} (\Gamma^{\nu e W^+,L}_{a, i} m_{e_{{i}}} (-2 \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^- ,R}_{c, a} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{\nu_{{a}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^- ,L}_{c, a} (1 + 2 I_2) m_{e_{{c}}}) + \Gamma^{\nu e W^+,R}_{a, i} (\Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^- ,R}_{c, a} (1 + 2 I_2) m^2_{e_{{i}}} - 2 \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^- ,L}_{c, a} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{\nu_{{a}}} m_{e_{{c}}})))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}})) \\ 
  PSO4lSLR= & -(( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,L}_{j, c, p} \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,R}_{l, k, p} \frac{1}{m^2_{h_{{p}}}} (\Gamma^{\nu e W^+,R}_{a, i} m_{e_{{i}}} (-2 \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^- ,L}_{c, a} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{\nu_{{a}}} + \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^- ,R}_{c, a} (1 + 2 I_2) m_{e_{{c}}}) + \Gamma^{\nu e W^+,L}_{a, i} (\Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^- ,L}_{c, a} (1 + 2 I_2) m^2_{e_{{i}}} - 2 \Gamma^{\bar{e}\nu W^- ,R}_{c, a} (1 - 2 I_1) m_{\nu_{{a}}} m_{e_{{c}}})))/(m^2_{e_{{i}}} - m^2_{e_{{c}}})) \\

\begin{align} 
I_1= & B_0(0, m^2_{\nu_{{a}}}, m^2_{W_R^-}) \\

  PSO4lTLL= & -( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,L}_{a, i, b} \Gamma^{e e \delta^{c++},L}_{k, a, c} \Gamma^{h \delta^{c--} \delta^{c++}}_{b, c, p} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\bar{e}\delta^{c--} ,L}_{l, j, p} \frac{1}{m^2_{\delta^{c--}_{{p}}}} I_1 m_{e_{{a}}})/8 \\ 
  PSO4lTLR= & 0 \\ 
  PSO4lTRL= & 0 \\ 
  PSO4lTRR= & -( \Gamma^{\bar{e}e h ,R}_{a, i, b} \Gamma^{e e \delta^{c++},R}_{k, a, c} \Gamma^{h \delta^{c--} \delta^{c++}}_{b, c, p} \Gamma^{\bar{e}\bar{e}\delta^{c--} ,R}_{l, j, p} \frac{1}{m^2_{\delta^{c--}_{{p}}}} I_1 m_{e_{{a}}})/8 \\ 
\end{align}
